FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreationDate], [p].[CreatorId], [p].[Description], [p].[Images], [p].[PostStatusId], [p].[Title], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[Avatar], [a].[BirthDate], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[Gender], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[Name], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreationDate] AS [CreationDate0], [c].[Title] AS [Title0]

    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]

    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[CommentBody], [c0].[CreationDate], [c0].[CreatorId], [c0].[PostId], [a0].[Id] AS [Id0], [a0].[AccessFailedCount], [a0].[Avatar], [a0].[BirthDate], [a0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a0].[Email], [a0].[EmailConfirmed], [a0].[Gender], [a0].[LockoutEnabled], [a0].[LockoutEnd], [a0].[Name], [a0].[NormalizedEmail], [a0].[NormalizedUserName], [a0].[PasswordHash], [a0].[PhoneNumber], [a0].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a0].[SecurityStamp], [a0].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a0].[UserName]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreationDate], [p].[CreatorId], [p].[Description], [p].[Images], [p].[PostStatusId], [p].[Title], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[Avatar], [a].[BirthDate], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[Gender], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[Name], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreationDate] AS [CreationDate0], [c].[Title] AS [Title0]
    FROM [Post] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [p].[CreatorId] = [a].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Category] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[CommentBody], [c0].[CreationDate], [c0].[CreatorId], [c0].[PostId], [a0].[Id] AS [Id0], [a0].[AccessFailedCount], [a0].[Avatar], [a0].[BirthDate], [a0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a0].[Email], [a0].[EmailConfirmed], [a0].[Gender], [a0].[LockoutEnabled], [a0].[LockoutEnd], [a0].[Name], [a0].[NormalizedEmail], [a0].[NormalizedUserName], [a0].[PasswordHash], [a0].[PhoneNumber], [a0].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a0].[SecurityStamp], [a0].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a0].[UserName]
    FROM [Comment] AS [c0]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a0] ON [c0].[CreatorId] = [a0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[PostId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
